\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_DEVICE\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_DEVICE\_CTX}!videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}}\index{videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_DEVICE\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_DEVICE\_CTX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba680870b80f0ed65e9ba97ea0905eb2fa}\label{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba680870b80f0ed65e9ba97ea0905eb2fa}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_acf8113e490f9e7b57465e65af9c0c75c}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+device\+\_\+ctx}} should have been set to a device of the specified type before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}!videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}}\index{videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}!AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX@{AV\_CODEC\_HW\_CONFIG\_METHOD\_HW\_FRAMES\_CTX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}\label{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55ba5a73dc7ff24a0b8ed69e2673d026ca11}} 
A\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+D\+E\+C\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+\+M\+E\+T\+H\+O\+D\+\_\+\+H\+W\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+S\+\_\+\+C\+TX&The codec supports this format via the hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx interface.

When selecting this format for a decoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to a suitable frames context inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{doc_2examples_2qsvdec_8c_afe1023087c26d2d410c9cd7d491c8660}{get\+\_\+format()}} callback. The frames context must have been created on a device of the specified type.

When selecting this format for an encoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to the context which will be used for the input frames before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\
\hline

This format can be selected without any additional configuration -\/ no device or frames context is required. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{ACB\_TYPE\_ASYMMETRIC@{ACB\_TYPE\_ASYMMETRIC}!videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}}\index{videotoolboxenc.c@{videotoolboxenc.c}!ACB\_TYPE\_ASYMMETRIC@{ACB\_TYPE\_ASYMMETRIC}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55bac4700fffa45f4445bf08f90e8eb55c14}\label{videotoolboxenc_8c_gga06fc87d81c62e9abb8790b6e5713c55bac4700fffa45f4445bf08f90e8eb55c14}} 
A\+C\+B\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+A\+S\+Y\+M\+M\+E\+T\+R\+IC&adaptive codebook with per-\/frame pitch, which we interpolate to get a per-\/sample pitch. Signal is generated using an asymmetric sinc window function \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{wmavoice__data_8h_a0c63d641283610a00b9b82d869b89ea2}{wmavoice\+\_\+ipol1\+\_\+coeffs}} 
\end{DoxyNote}

A\+V\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+R\+O\+P\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+L\+I\+G\+N\+ED&Apply the maximum possible cropping, even if it requires setting the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}}\mbox{[}\mbox{]} entries to unaligned pointers. Passing unaligned data to F\+Fmpeg A\+PI is generally not allowed, and causes undefined behavior (such as crashes). You can pass unaligned data only to F\+Fmpeg A\+P\+Is that are explicitly documented to accept it. Use this flag only if you absolutely know what you are doing. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} copy\+\_\+emulation\+\_\+prev (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+\_\+size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{ssize\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+offset,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Copies the data inserting emulation prevention bytes as needed. Existing data in the destination can be taken into account by providing dst with a dst\+\_\+offset $>$ 0.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of bytes copied on success. On failure, the negative of the number of bytes needed to copy src is returned. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{copy\_replace\_length\_codes()}{copy\_replace\_length\_codes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} copy\+\_\+replace\+\_\+length\+\_\+codes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{avctx,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length\+\_\+code\+\_\+size,  }\item[{C\+M\+Sample\+Buffer\+Ref}]{sample\+\_\+buffer,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_extra_s_e_i}{Extra\+S\+EI}} $\ast$}]{sei,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{dst\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Copies N\+AL units and replaces length codes with H.\+264 Annex B start codes. On failure, the contents of dst\+\_\+data may have been modified.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em length\+\_\+code\+\_\+size} & Byte length of each length code \\
\hline
{\em sample\+\_\+buffer} & N\+AL units prefixed with length codes. \\
\hline
{\em sei} & Optional A53 closed captions S\+EI data. \\
\hline
{\em dst\+\_\+data} & Must be zeroed before calling this function. Contains the copied N\+AL units prefixed with start codes when the function returns successfully. \\
\hline
{\em dst\+\_\+size} & Length of dst\+\_\+data \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+I\+D\+D\+A\+TA if length\+\_\+code\+\_\+size is invalid A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+S\+M\+A\+LL if dst\+\_\+data is too small or if a length\+\_\+code in src\+\_\+data specifies data beyond the end of its buffer. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} get\+\_\+params\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} $\ast$}]{avctx,  }\item[{C\+M\+Video\+Format\+Description\+Ref}]{vid\+\_\+fmt,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Get the parameter sets from a C\+M\+Sample\+Buffer\+Ref. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst} & If $\ast$dst isn\textquotesingle{}t N\+U\+LL, the parameters are copied into existing memory. $\ast$dst\+\_\+size must be set accordingly when $\ast$dst != N\+U\+LL. If $\ast$dst is N\+U\+LL, it will be allocated. In all cases, $\ast$dst\+\_\+size is set to the number of bytes used starting at $\ast$dst. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
